GT Equivalence Verification (BPG16)
============================================================
GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P**c6 + c7*P
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is a fixed function of **P only** (no dependence on *t*):
\[
0.86778\cdot(-1+P/6.0579)\cdot(1-P/14.1851)\cdot P\;+\;0.86778\,P^{1/3}\;+\;0.86778\,P.
\]
Expanding the first product shows GT contains a **cubic polynomial in \(P\)** plus a **non-polynomial term \(P^{1/3}\)**:
\[
\text{GT}(P)=a_3P^3+a_2P^2+a_1P + a_{1/3}P^{1/3},
\]
with \(a_{1/3}=0.86778\neq 0\).  
So any matching candidate must (i) be independent of \(t\) after parameter choice, and (ii) be able to produce an explicit \(P^{1/3}\) term (not via logs/exp/rationals unless they can reduce exactly to \(P^{1/3}\) for all \(P\), which they cannot).

Below, for each candidate, I check whether (A) all \(t\)-dependence can be removed by setting coefficients to 0, and (B) whether the remaining \(P\)-dependence can equal “cubic polynomial + \(P^{1/3}\)”.

### 1.

### 22.

### 23.
Has \(P^{c3}c4\) plus tanh(t) and constant. Set tanh coefficient \(c5=0\) and constant \(c8=0\). Then expression is polynomial + \(c4 P^{c3}\). This *could* create \(P^{1/3}\) by choosing \(c3=1/3\) and \(c4=0.86778\).  
But GT also has a specific cubic polynomial part. Candidate 23 has independent \(P^3, P^2, P\) coefficients (via \(c0,c1,c2,c3\)?? careful: here \(c3\) is exponent, so polynomial part is \(P^3 c0 + P^2 c1 + P c2\) only). GT’s polynomial part includes **\(P^3,P^2,P\)** only (no constant), so that part can be matched by choosing \(c0,c1,c2\) appropriately. Therefore candidate 23 **can** match GT exactly:
- set tanh term off: \(c5=0\)
- set constant off: \(c8=0\)
- set power term: \(c3=1/3,\; c4=0.8677806610632854\)
- set polynomial coefficients \(c0,c1,c2\) to equal GT’s cubic/quadratic/linear coefficients from expanding the first product plus the extra \(+0.86778 P\) (absorbed into linear coefficient).
So **this one is a potential match**.

To be sure: GT polynomial part is cubic with no other non-polynomial terms besides \(P^{1/3}\). Candidate 23 provides exactly “cubic + quadratic + linear + \(P^{c3}\)” after zeroing tanh/constant. That matches the GT structure perfectly. **Match possible.**

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG16)
============================================================
GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P**c6 + c7*P
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: [13, 23]
Matched candidates: ["P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P**2*c2 + P*c3 + P**c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*exp(c8/(c9 + t))", "P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2 + P**c3*c4 + c5*tanh(c6*t + c7) + c8"]

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare it with each candidate.

**GT expression (simplified):**
```
0.8678*(-1 + P/6.058)*(1 - P/14.185)*P + 0.8678*P^(1/3) + 0.8678*P
```

Let me expand the polynomial part:
(-1 + P/6.058)*(1 - P/14.185) = -1 + P/14.185 + P/6.058 - P²/(6.058*14.185)

So the first term times P:
= -P + P²/14.185 + P²/6.058 - P³/(6.058*14.185)

Multiplied by 0.8678:
= -0.8678*P + 0.8678*P²/14.185 + 0.8678*P²/6.058 - 0.8678*P³/85.91

Adding the remaining terms:
+ 0.8678*P^(1/3) + 0.8678*P

The -0.8678*P and +0.8678*P cancel!

**GT = c_a*P³ + c_b*P² + 0.8678*P^(1/3)**

where c_a = -0.8678/(6.058*14.185) and c_b = 0.8678*(1/14.185 + 1/6.058)

So GT has three basis functions: **P³, P², P^(1/3)** with NO dependence on t.

Key features of GT:
1. P³ term (cubic)
2. P² term (quadratic)  
3. P^(1/3) term (cube root)
4. **No linear P term** (they cancelled)
5. **No t dependence**
6. **No constant term**

Now I'll check each candidate. For candidates with t-dependence, I need the coefficient of t-dependent terms to be 0. For P^(1/3), I need that specific basis function.

Let me systematically check which candidates can produce P³ + P² + P^(1/3) with no other terms:

**Candidates with P^(1/3) or P^c term:** Only candidates 23, 38, 35, 48, 17, 13, 30 have power-law terms like P^c.

**Candidate 23:** P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + P^c3 * c4 + c5*tanh(c6*t+c7) + c8
- Set c5=0 (kill tanh), c2=0 (kill P), c3=1/3, then: P³c0 + P²c1 + c4*P^(1/3) + c8
- But there's a constant c8. GT has no constant. Set c8=0.
- Result: P³c0 + P²c1 + c4*P^(1/3) ✓

**Candidate 23 verdict: [MATCH]**

**Candidate 38:** P²c0 + P*P^c1*c2 + Pc3 + Pc4 + c5*tanh(c6*t+c7)
- P*P^c1 = P^(1+c1). Set c1 = -2/3, get P^(1/3). But no P³ term. Missing cubic. 
**Candidate 38 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 30:** P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + c3*tanh(c4*t+c5) + c6*log(P^c7*c8+1)
- log term ≠ P^(1/3). **Candidate 30 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 35:** P³c0 + P²c1 + P²c2 + Pc3 + Pc4 + c5*t/(c6+t²) + c7*(Pc8+1)^c9
- Set c5=0, c3+c4=0. (Pc8+1)^c9 with c9=1/3 gives (Pc8+1)^(1/3) ≠ P^(1/3).
**Candidate 35 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

For all other candidates without a P^(1/3) or equivalent fractional power basis function, they cannot match GT. Let me verify candidates 13, 17, 48:

**Candidate 13:** Has P^c4*c5*exp(c6*t). Set c6=0: P^c4*c5. Set c4=1/3. But also has exp(c7/(c8+t)) - set this to constant? exp(c7/(c8+t)) varies with t unless c7=0, giving constant 1. Then: P³c0+P²(c1+c2)+Pc3+c5*P^(1/3)+c7_const. Set c3=0, c7=0 effectively. Result: P³+P²+P^(1/3) ✓
**Candidate 13 verdict: [MATCH]**

**Candidate 48:** P^c4*c5*exp(c6*t) - set c6=0, c4=1/3. But has P*c2*exp(Pc3) which can't be zeroed without losing needed terms unless c2=0. Missing P³. **Candidate 48 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 17:** P^c5*c6*log(Pc7+1) ≠ P^(1/3). **Candidate 17 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

Going through remaining candidates (1-22, 24-29, 31-34, 36-37, 39-50): None have a free P^c power term, so none can produce P^(1/3).

Candidates 1-12,14-16,18-22,24-29,31-34,36-37,39-47,49-50: **[NO MATCH]**

Matched candidate IDs: [13, 23]
